Advantages of decentralized systems
‚ùñ Fault tolerance
‚ùñ Independence from individual control
‚ùñ Trustless (no need to trust a third party)
‚ùñ Permissionless (free use)
‚ùñ Persistence (immutability of the final state of a database)
‚ùñ Liveness (appending records is guaranteed)
‚ùñ Formality of protocols
